Now I see what's happening. Looking at the test file (line 316), the expected format for passing cookies through gRPC metadata is:```\n\"grpcgateway-cookie\": []string{\"flipt_client_token=\" + clientToken}\n```\n\nBut the `ForwardCookies` function in `internal/server/authn/method/http.go` is not setting the cookies in the `grpcgateway-cookie` header format. It's just setting them directly in the metadata with the cookie key names.\n\nNow let me understand the two bugs:\n\n1. **Cookie Token Not Extracted**: The `ForwardCookies` function (line 45-54 in http.go) has a bug on line 49. It always puts the cookie value into the metadata with the key `stateCookieKey` instead of the actual `key` variable. This means when iterating:\n   - First iteration: `key = stateCookieKey`, stores in `md[stateCookieKey]` ✓\n   - Second iteration: `key = tokenCookieKey`, stores in `md[stateCookieKey]` instead of `md[tokenCookieKey]` ✗\n\n   This causes the token cookie to be overwritten or lost.\n\n2. Additionally, even if that bug was fixed, the metadata format might not match what's expected in the gRPC middleware. The `cookieFromMetadata` function expects the cookies to be in the `grpcgateway-cookie` header as a full cookie string like `\"flipt_client_token=value\"`.\n\n2. **Server-level Authentication Bypass**: Looking at the gRPC middleware (lines 82-95 in middleware.go), there's a mechanism to skip authentication using the `SkipsAuthenticationServer` interface or a list of `skippedServers`. However, when using the HTTP/REST API through gRPC gateway, there's no way to configure a server instance to skip authentication at the HTTP layer.\n\n   The HTTP middleware (internal/server/authn/middleware/http/middleware.go) doesn't have an equivalent skip mechanism. It only handles clearing cookies on logout and error handling.\n   \nI should write tests to expose these issues. w.Code)\n\n\t\t// The test demonstrates that while the browser properly sends the token\n\t\t// in a cookie, the authentication system fails to properly extract it\n\t\t// and forward it to the gRPC AuthenticationConfig struct {\n39: \t// Required designates whether authentication credentials are validated.\n40: \t// If required == true, then authentication is required for all API endpoints.\n41: \t// Else, authentication is not required and Flipt's APIs are not secured.\n42: \tRequired bool `json:\"required\" mapstructure:\"required\" yaml:\"required\"`\n43: \n44: \t// Exclude allows you to skip enforcing authentication on the different\n45: \t// top-level sections of the API.\n46: \t// By default, given required == true, the API is fully protected.\n47: \tExclude struct {\n48: \t\t// Management refers to the section of the API with the prefix /api/v1\n49: \t\tManagement bool `json:\"management,omitempty\" mapstructure:\"management\" yaml:\"management,omitempty\"`\n50: \t\t// Metadata refers to the section of the API with the prefix /meta\n51: \t\tMetadata bool `json:\"metadata,omitempty\" mapstructure:\"metadata\" yaml:\"metadata,omitempty\"`\n52: \t\t// Evaluation refers to the section of the API with the prefix /evaluation/v1\n53: \t\tEvaluation bool `json:\"evaluation,omitempty\" mapstructure:\"evaluation\" yaml:\"evaluation,omitempty\"`\n54: \t} `json:\"exclude,omitempty\" mapstructure:\"exclude\" yaml:\"exclude,omitempty\"`\n55: \n56: \tSession AuthenticationSession `json:\"session,omitempty\" mapstructure:\"session\" yaml:\"session,omitempty\"`\n57: \tMethods AuthenticationMethods `json:\"methods,omitempty\" mapstructure:\"methods\" yaml:\"methods,omitempty\"`\n58: }\n59: \n60: // Enabled returns true if authentication is marked as required\n61: // or any of the authentication methods are enabled.\n62: func (c AuthenticationConfig) Enabled() bool {\n63: \tif c.Required {\n64: \t\treturn true\n65: \t}\n66: \n67: \tfor _, info := range c.Methods.AllMethods() {\n68: \t\tif info.Enabled {\n69: \t\t\treturn true\n70: \t\t}\n71: \t}\n72: \n73: \treturn false\n74: }\n75: \n76: // RequiresDatabase returns true if any of the enabled authentication\n77: // methods requires a database connection\n78: func (c AuthenticationConfig) RequiresDatabase() bool {\n79: \tfor _, info := range c.Methods.AllMethods() {\n80: \t\tif info.Enabled && info.RequiresDatabase {\n81: \t\t\treturn true\n82: \t\t}\n83: \t}\n84: \n85: \treturn false\n86: }\n87: \n88: // IsZero returns true if the authentication config is not enabled.\n89: // This is used for marshalling to YAML for `config init`.\n90: func (c AuthenticationConfig) IsZero() bool {\n91: \treturn !c.Enabled()\n92: }\n93: \n94: // (non-nil).\n97: func (c AuthenticationConfig) ShouldRunCleanup() (shouldCleanup bool) {\n98: \tfor _, info := range c.Methods.AllMethods() {\n99: \t\tshouldCleanup = shouldCleanup || (info.Enabled && info.RequiresDatabase && info.Cleanup != nil)\n100: \t}\n101: \n102: \treturn\n103: }\n104: \n105: func (c *AuthenticationConfig) setDefaults(v *viper.Viper) error {\n106: \tmethods := {\n115: \t\t\t// apply any method specific defaults\n116: \t\t\tinfo.setDefaults(method)\n117: \t\t\t// set default cleanup\n118: \t\t\tmethod[\"cleanup\"] = map[string]any{\n119: \t\t\t\t\"interval\":     time.Hour,\n120: \t\t\t\t\"grace_period\": 30 * time.Minute,\n121: \t\t\t}\n122: \t\t}\n123: \n124: \t\tmethods[info.Name()] = method\n125: \t}\n126: \n127: \tv.SetDefault(\"authentication\", map[string]any{\n128: \t\t\"required\": false,\n129: \t\t\"session\": map[string]any{\n130: \t\t\t\"token_lifetime\": \"24h\",\n131: \t\t\t\"state_lifetime\": \"10m\",\n132: \t\t},\n133: \t\t\"methods\": methods,\n134: \t})\n135: \n136: \treturn nil\n137: }\n138: \n139: func (c *AuthenticationConfig) SessionEnabled() bool {\n140: \tvar sessionEnabled bool\n141: \tfor _, info := range c.Methods.AllMethods() {\n142: \t\tsessionEnabled = sessionEnabled || (info.Enabled && info.SessionCompatible)\n143: \t}\n144: \n145: \treturn sessionEnabled\n146: }\n147: \n148: func (c *AuthenticationConfig) validate() error {\n149: \tvar sessionEnabled bool\n150: \n151: \tfor _, info := range c.Methods.AllMethods() {\n152: \t\tsessionEnabled = sessionEnabled || (info.Enabled && info.SessionCompatible)\n153: \t\tif info.Cleanup == nil {\n154: \t\t\tcontinue\n155: \t\t}\n156: \n157: \t\tfield := \"authentication.method\" + info.Name()\n158: \t\tif info.Cleanup.Interval <= 0 {\n159: \t\t\treturn errFieldWrap(field+\".cleanup.interval\", errPositiveNonZeroDuration)\n160: \t\t}\n161: \n162: \t\tif info.Cleanup.GracePeriod <= 0 {\n163: \t\t\treturn errFieldWrap(field+\".cleanup.grace_period\", errPositiveNonZeroDuration)\n164: \t\t}\n165: \t}\n166: \n167: \t// ensure that when a session compatible authentication method has been\n168: \t// getHostname(c.Session.Domain)\n177: \t\tif err != nil {\n178: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid domain: %w\", err)\n179: \t\t}\n180: \n181: \t\t// strip scheme and port from domain\n182: \t\t// domain cookies are not allowed to have a scheme or port\n183: \t\t// https://github.com/golang/go/issues/28297\n184: \t\tc.Session.Domain = host\n185: \t}\n186: \n187: \tfor _, info := range c.Methods.AllMethods() {\n188: \t\tif err := info.validate(); err != nil {\n189: \t\t\treturn err\n190: \t\t}\n191: \t}\n192: \n193: \treturn nil\n194: }\n195: \n196: func (c *AuthenticationConfig) \treturn nil\n202: }\n203: \n204: func getHostname(rawurl string) (string, error) {\n205: \tif !strings.Contains(rawurl, \"://\") {\n206: \t\trawurl = \"http://\" + rawurl\n207: \t}\n208: \tu, err := \n571: \treturn nil\n572: }\n573: \n574: type AuthenticationMethodJWTConfig struct {\n575: \t// ValidateClaims is used to validate the claims of the JWT token.\n576: \tValidateClaims struct {\n577:
